# Platform Knowledge: Flink Windowing API Extension Points

## Your Task

Map the extension points in Apache Flink's windowing API that a developer would need to implement a custom window assigner. Find: 1. The abstract base class `WindowAssigner` in `flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/` — report its abstract methods. 2. The `MergingWindowAssigner` subclass that adds `mergeWindows()` for session-style windows. 3. The `Trigger` base class in the triggers package — report the lifecycle methods (`onElement`, `onEventTime`, `onProcessingTime`, `onMerge`). 4. An existing reference implementation: `EventTimeSessionWindows` — report how it implements `assignWindows()` and `mergeWindows()`. 5. The `TimeWindow` class that concrete assigners produce. For each, report the file path, class name, and key method signatures.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the platform domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kafka--0753c489, sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc, sg-evals/camel--1006f047.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/kafka--0753c489` (apache/kafka)
- `sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc` (apache/flink)
- `sg-evals/camel--1006f047` (apache/camel)

Perfect! I've successfully documented the Apache Flink windowing API extension points. Here's a summary of what was found:

## Key Findings

**1. WindowAssigner (Base Extension Point)**
- Location: `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/WindowAssigner.java`
- 4 abstract methods to implement: `assignWindows()`, `getDefaultTrigger()`, `getWindowSerializer()`, `isEventTime()`

**2. MergingWindowAssigner (Session Window Support)**
- Location: `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/MergingWindowAssigner.java`
- Adds abstract method: `mergeWindows(Collection<W> windows, MergeCallback<W> callback)`

**3. Trigger (Lifecycle Callbacks)**
- Location: `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/triggers/Trigger.java`
- 4 core abstract methods: `onElement()`, `onProcessingTime()`, `onEventTime()`, `clear()`
- Optional merging methods: `canMerge()`, `onMerge()`

**4. EventTimeSessionWindows (Reference Implementation)**
- Location: `flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/EventTimeSessionWindows.java`
- Implements `assignWindows()` to create single TimeWindow per element
- Implements `mergeWindows()` using TimeWindow.mergeWindows() utility

**5. TimeWindow (Window Representation)**
- Location: `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/windows/TimeWindow.java`
- Represents time interval from inclusive start to exclusive end
- Provides utility methods for merging overlapping windows

The complete answer with detailed method signatures and implementation details has been written to `/workspace/answer.json`.

WindowAssigner (Base Class)\\n**Location:** flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/WindowAssigner.java\\n\\n**Class:** `public abstract class WindowAssigner<T, W extends Window> implements Serializable`\\n\\n**Abstract Methods (Extension Points):**\\n- `public abstract Collection<W> assignWindows(T element, long timestamp, WindowAssignerContext context)` - Called to assign zero or more windows to an incoming element\\n- `public abstract Trigger<T, W> getDefaultTrigger()` - Returns the default trigger for this window assigner\\n- `public abstract TypeSerializer<W> getWindowSerializer(ExecutionConfig executionConfig)` - Returns a serializer for windows produced by this assigner\\n- `public abstract boolean isEventTime()` - Returns true if windows are based on event time, false for processing time\\n\\n## 2. MergingWindowAssigner (Subclass for Session Windows)\\n**Location:** flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/MergingWindowAssigner.java\\n\\n**Class:** `public abstract class MergingWindowAssigner<T, W extends Window> extends WindowAssigner<T, W>`\\n\\n**Additional Abstract Method:**\\n- `public abstract void mergeWindows(Collection<W> windows, MergeCallback<W> callback)` - Determines which windows should be merged and invokes the callback to signal the merge operations\\n\\n**Supporting Interface:**\\n- `MergeCallback<W>` with method `void merge(Collection<W> toBeMerged, W mergeResult)` - Called to merge windows\\n\\n## 3. Trigger (Lifecycle Callback Base Class)\\n**Location:** flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/triggers/Trigger.java\\n\\n**Class:** `public abstract class Trigger<T, W extends Window> implements Serializable`\\n\\n**Core Lifecycle Methods (Abstract):**\\n- `public abstract TriggerResult onElement(T element, long timestamp, W window, TriggerContext ctx) throws Exception` - Called when an element is added to a pane\\n- `public abstract TriggerResult onProcessingTime(long time, W window, TriggerContext ctx) throws Exception` - Called when a processing-time timer fires\\n- `public abstract TriggerResult onEventTime(long time, W window, TriggerContext ctx) throws Exception` - Called when an event-time timer fires\\n- `public abstract void clear(W window, TriggerContext ctx) throws Exception` - Called when a window is purged to clean up state\\n\\n**Merging-Related Methods (Optional):**\\n- `public boolean canMerge()` - Returns false by default; override to return true if trigger supports merging\\n- `public void onMerge(W window, OnMergeContext ctx) throws Exception` - Called when windows are merged; must be overridden if canMerge() returns true\\n\\n## 4. EventTimeSessionWindows (Reference Implementation)\\n**Location:** flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/EventTimeSessionWindows.java\\n\\n**Class:** `public class EventTimeSessionWindows extends MergingWindowAssigner<Object, TimeWindow>`\\n\\n**Key Implementation Details:**\\n- **assignWindows()** - Creates a single TimeWindow for each element: `return Collections.singletonList(new TimeWindow(timestamp, timestamp + sessionTimeout));`\\n- **mergeWindows()** - Delegates to TimeWindow utility: `TimeWindow.mergeWindows(windows, c);`\\n- **getDefaultTrigger()** - Returns `EventTimeTrigger.create()`\\n- **isEventTime()** - Returns `true`\\n- Constructor accepts `long sessionTimeout` parameter defining the session gap\\n\\n## 5. TimeWindow (Window Representation)\\n**Location:** flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/windows/TimeWindow.java\\n\\n**Class:** `public class TimeWindow extends Window`\\n\\n**Core Structure:**\\n- Constructor: `public TimeWindow(long start, long end)` - Creates window with inclusive start and exclusive end\\n- `public long getStart()` - Returns inclusive start timestamp\\n- `public long getEnd()` - Returns exclusive end timestamp\\n- `public long maxTimestamp()` - Returns `end - 1` (largest inclusive timestamp)\\n- `public boolean intersects(TimeWindow other)` - Checks if windows overlap or touch\\n- `public TimeWindow cover(TimeWindow other)` - Returns minimal window covering both windows\\n\\n**Utility Methods:**\\n- `public static void mergeWindows(Collection<TimeWindow> windows, MergingWindowAssigner.MergeCallback<TimeWindow> c)` - Merges overlapping windows by sorting and grouping\\n- `public static long getWindowStartWithOffset(long timestamp, long offset, long windowSize)` - Calculates window start for tumbling/sliding windows\\n\\n## Extension Point Chain\\nTo implement a custom window assigner, developers follow this pattern:\\n1. Extend `WindowAssigner` (or `MergingWindowAssigner` for session-style windows)\\n2. Implement `assignWindows()` to create TimeWindow instances\\n3. For merging assigners, implement `mergeWindows()` to determine which windows should merge\\n4. Optionally extend `Trigger` to implement custom trigger logic with lifecycle callbacks\\n5. Specify the trigger via `getDefaultTrigger()` or override at usage time\\n\\nThe `EventTimeSessionWindows` class demonstrates this pattern: it extends `MergingWindowAssigner`, creates `TimeWindow` objects with gap-based logic, and reuses `TimeWindow.mergeWindows()` for window merging logic.\"\n}\n",
